earlier than `created_at` (can't submit before record creation)\n    53→- Future dates (timestamps beyond the current date)\n    54→- Unreasonably fast approvals (e.g. approved_at within seconds of submitted_at)\n    55→\n    56→### Missing Required Fields\n    57→- Projects without a `title`\n    58→- Projects without an `ahj_id` or with an `ahj_id` that doesn't exist in the `ahjs` table\n    59→- Projects with empty or null `status`\n    60→- Projects with unrecognised `status` values (not in: draft, submitted, approved, revision_required)\n    61→- Projects with unrecognised `project_type_id` values\n    62→\n    63→### Cross-AHJ Analysis\n    64→- Report counts per AHJ separately\n    65→- Flag if any projects reference a non-existent AHJ\n    66→\n    67→## Report private function generateReport()\n    {\n        $totalIssues = count($this->criticalIssues) + count($this->warningIssues) + count($this->infoIssues);\n        $totalProjects = Project::count();\n        \n        $ahjBreakdown = $this->getAhjBreakdown();\n        \n        $report = \"# Data Integrity Report\\n\";\n        $report .= \"Generated: \" . Per-AHJ Breakdown\\n\";\n            foreach ($ahjBreakdown as $ahjName => $counts) {\n                $report .= \"- **{$ahjName}**: {$counts['total']} issues (Critical: {$counts['critical']}, (!empty($this->criticalIssues)) {\n            $report .= \"### Critical\\n\";\n            $report .= \"_Issues that would cause application errors or data corruption_\\n\\n\";\n            foreach
